msg:The hotel is in a great location, next to the forest park, surrounded by water systems, very cozy and quiet. The hotel itself is in a garden style. It is very comfortable to drink tea and meet friends by the river. The service is very good. The service staff are well-trained and will greet politely. The check-in efficiency is very high and they will respond to any request.
It is so nice to have a bowl of noodles by the river for breakfast. I like chicken soup noodles very much, a piece of braised meat, a portion of shrimp, and free ginger and garlic leaves to keep you energetic all day!
The room is very new and high-end, with a capsule coffee machine, a self-service water dispenser, a large bathroom with dry and wet separation, and a bathtub. The gym is very suitable for fitness on rainy days, but you can take a walk in the park on sunny days. There is also a self-service laundry room on the first floor, which is very considerate. Washing, drying and drying are all solved. It is the place I like most when I travel on business.
The hotel is lush and green. It just happened that the hotel was trimming the greenery and the lawns were all renewed. It can be seen that the hotel is extremely attentive. The underground parking lot is also clean and tidy, parking is orderly, and the signs are clear at a glance. ğŸ‘ğŸ‘ğŸ‘
Sunshine Peninsula Hotel is my favorite hotel, no doubt about it. I have recommended it to my colleagues in the company and it is the first choice for future business trips.
